#
# TABLE STRUCTURE FOR: remoutless
#

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `remoutless`;

CREATE TABLE `remoutless` (
  `id` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `remoutless` enum('very hot','hot','warm','cold','very cold') COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=6 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_unicode_ci;

INSERT INTO `remoutless` (`id`, `remoutless`) VALUES (1, 'very cold');
INSERT INTO `remoutless` (`id`, `remoutless`) VALUES (2, 'cold');
INSERT INTO `remoutless` (`id`, `remoutless`) VALUES (3, 'very hot');
INSERT INTO `remoutless` (`id`, `remoutless`) VALUES (4, 'warm');
INSERT INTO `remoutless` (`id`, `remoutless`) VALUES (5, 'hot');
